# Kimi Guided Reading Unique Word Audio Request

Generate one MP3 per unique Guided Reading word only. Do not generate duplicates for repeated words.

## Global Voice Requirements

- One consistent voice across all files.
- Neutral soft light female voice.
- American English.
- Gentle but not babyish.
- Clean studio-style audio.
- No background noise.
- No music.
- No effects.
- No leading spoken instructions.
- No trailing commentary.
- Say only the target word.
- Do not say "slowly and clearly".
- Do not say file names.
- Do not say quotation marks.
- Do not spell the word.

## Files To Generate

### 1

- Word: 1
- Slug: 1
- Destination path: `public/guided-reading/audio/words/1.mp3`
- Request: Record clear American English MP3 saying only "1", no sentence, no spelling, no music, no effects, neutral soft light female voice, child-friendly K-2 pronunciation.
- Review flags: number
